name:H‚ÄçA‚ÄçP‚ÄçP‚ÄçI‚ÄçN‚ÄçE‚ÄçS‚ÄçS‚Äç_‚ÄçB‚Äço
info:Business Queen Room
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:39 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted May 21, 2024
msg:I made a temporary arrangement during the May Day holiday and looked through my hotel collection. I have never been to CITIC Jinling Hotel. There was a room available on the date. I did not book it at the beginning of the holiday, but at the last two days of the holiday. I went there for a rest and mainly stayed in a hotel.
The hotel is surrounded by mountains on three sides, with a reservoir in front. There are entrances and exits in the hotel building that can lead directly to the outside. Because it is built on the mountain, the highest floor of the hotel is at the top of the mountain behind, and there are electric cars available for payment, which is very friendly to the elderly and children.
There is a children's playground, cinema, billiard hall, swimming pool, gym in the building..., and a poplar forest, botanical garden (not big), outdoor nursery (consumption alone), karts... outside the building. There is also an observation deck and a small lake in front of the building (children like to play in the water here). Internet celebrity coffee shop, the scenery is very good, the price is slightly high, and the taste is average. There is Starbucks in the hotel lobby. During our stay, there was only American coffee, no other, the price is reasonable, and the brand is unified.
The hotel is hygienic. There is dust, and the dust on the desk of the lobby front desk is also obvious, but it can be felt that the original facilities are still good, but it has been a long time.
Children love buffets, so in addition to the standard breakfast buffet, the dinner on the first day was also a buffet in the restaurant on the first floor, and buffet coupons were provided when checking in. The whole family liked this place very much. Staying for one night was not enough to enjoy the whole thing, and at least two nights was the starting point. It is very suitable for family travel within Beijing.

msg:One day during the Ching Ming holiday, I took the children on an outing tour around Beijing.
This time we come to check in at the CITIC Jinling Hotel in Pinggu Mountain.
Packages purchased in advance, rooms reserved in advance. It's a pity that it was raining moderately in Beijing on the day we came. We drove for more than 2 hours from the Northwest Third Ring Road to get there, 100 kilometers, which is considered a relatively long distance.
The hotel has free parking. I feel that there are not many parking spaces, and they are basically full.
The lady at the front desk, Chen Naijing, is very friendly. She saw that we were two big and two young and gave us a parent-child room. Thank you.
Room facilities:
The room is a bit old, but it still has everything that a parent-child room should have. The small items are cute, and the children like it very much. The minibar is basically charged, and everyone uses it on demand. However, the door of the room is not very soundproof. At night, I can clearly hear the rubbing sound of the suitcase and the ground when checking in next to me.
Room view:
The scenery outside the room is definitely five-star. The view after the new rain in the empty mountain is beautiful! However, both sides of the viewing platform are leaky, and the privacy is a little bit less.
I didn't go to the swimming pool and gym, but they are said to be pretty good.
Dining room:
For dinner, we had a buffet at the western restaurant on the first floor, 168 people. Although there are no big dishes, it is no problem to be full. There are some special dishes of Jiangsu. Although they cannot be said to be amazing, they are still okay. There are not many people, and you can eat quietly.
Breakfast on the second day was also at the western restaurant on the first floor, because there were more people in the room, and it also had some Jiangsu flavors, and the Yangchun noodles tasted quite authentic.
The next day we had lunch at the Huaiyangzao Chinese restaurant on the fifth floor. We ate limited dishes in the set menu. The reviews said that it was not very tasty, so we didn‚Äôt report our expectations, but we thought it was okay. Especially Yangzhou fried rice, the ingredients are very rich, and the children like it very much.
There are a large group of geese and fish in the lake in the hotel, which can be fed, but the rabbit mentioned before is gone, and it is said that it was killed by other animals. . .
The next morning we went to see the small tropical rainforest that comes with the hotel. It was very small, and we walked around for five minutes, just to take the children for a walk. There are many flowers blooming along the way, and it is very suitable for taking pictures with the distant mountains and rivers.
The set meal brings a catty of strawberry picking, which is also in the hotel's park. The boss is very nice. An aunt helped us find red and ripe strawberries, and let us taste them casually. Not to mention, the taste is not bad, and the children like it too, so we don‚Äôt care too much about it.
In the afternoon, we went to experience the open-air children's playground in the hotel park - Mowang Paradise. Tickets are 168. Our two children get one in the package. In fact, there is also a small free playground in the hotel, but it is too small, not ventilated, and has a strange smell. . Don't let the children play for too long. Magic Net Paradise is mainly composed of rainbow slides and magic nets. It is suitable for children's shoes aged 5 to 12. There are also some sandpit and basketball shoes. It is definitely no problem for children to play all afternoon, and the price is a bit expensive. After all It's in the hotel.
Overall, it exceeded my expectations. It is suitable for parent-child vacations, the air environment is good, and it is also good for the elderly to recuperate.

Dining in the outskirts is already very good. After tasting the evening buffet and breakfast, it must be incomparable with the five-star hotels in the city, but the price is not expensive. There are all the things that should be there, which is already very good. I am very satisfied.

The swimming pool is great, much larger than other five-star hotels. We went there once more than eight in the morning, only two people. Went there once at 3 o'clock in the afternoon and there were more people.

The children's playground is also very good, and there is a small lake where children can fish for small fish or something. In short, it is worth it. recommend.

hotel:
1. The exterior of the hotel is peculiar. There is a viewing platform. In summer and autumn, you can enjoy the lake view and feed the fish and ducks. It should be a peculiar parent-child experience.
2. The rooms in the main building of the hotel are basically facing north. It is nothing more than a problem of more lake views or less lake views. If it is recommended to have a lake view room type, communicate with the reservation depar**ent in advance to ask for the middle position of the upper floors. .
3. This stay is a view room. After check-in, due to unexpected problems (will be described below), the suite was directly upgraded. The room type is very good, the panoramic view of the north lake, one living room and one bedroom, reasonable design, two toilets, if you bring the elderly, it will be very convenient.
4. The sanitation of the room is indeed average, and there will indeed be the situation that the cleaning mentioned in the comments is not clean. It is recommended that the hotel strengthen it.
5. In particular, the shower in the suite is very strange. There are too many buttons and the introduction is incomplete. The scale causes the spraying direction to be the same as the fireworks. It is recommended that you pay attention and study well before taking a shower.

Serve:
1. First, the doorman will not see you going out, and secondly, if he doesn't carry the suitcase for you, he will just sit at the entrance of the hall and wait for the guests to clean the health treasure.
2. There are few receptionists at the front desk, and the professionalism needs to be verified. As a Jinling Platinum member who matches a pig's F4, it stands to reason that the room should be upgraded. In the end, the room was not upgraded. The baby swiped the card to enter the room, and it turned out to be a room with guests, which is really strange. Fortunately, Li Xiaoling, the lobby manager at the front desk, took the initiative to upgrade me to a suite after understanding the situation in time. She was very professional, thank you very much!

food:
1. The hotel is far away from Pinggu County, except that the hotel restaurant is basically surrounded by farmhouses, and it may even catch up with the situation that too many farmhouses do not take orders during the meal time.
2. The taste of the hotel restaurant is quite satisfactory, not as amazing as other evaluations say. On the other hand, the 15% service fee for basically no service is very "stunning", with poor service awareness and poor service attitude. Only by drinking water and calling the waiters constantly can you make some money back. If you are a Jinling Platinum member matched by a pig F4, you can get a 12% discount.

entertainment:
1. Turn left at the entrance of the hotel lobby. The water is really cold, about 26 degrees, and the water quality is average. It feels like it is not filtered. It is not recommended for babies to go into the water.
2. The hot spring is 99 yuan for two people, medicine pool, 20 minutes, and it is not recommended for babies to go into the water. To sum up, playing with water is no fun.
3. The amusement park is really small, pocket-sized, and it feels only a few dozen square meters. It is not recommended for children to play with children of mixed ages.
4. The indoor tennis courts and badminton courts must be praised, and the conditions are very good. If the hotel package is included, choose one and one hour is enough to play.
5. The movies in the movie hall are not cartoons, the sound is low, and the indoor temperature is high. However, the hotel lobby is much colder in winter, so it is recommended to pay attention to dressing.
6. The botanical garden provided by the hotel is not big. It is behind the hotel. It can take ten minutes and no tickets are required. However, it is very considerate to have a small animal card in English.
7. Next to the botanical garden is an outdoor playground, which is very small and comparable to the scale of the community. The winter snow park is a bit like the facilities in the village. It is 128 yuan for two large and two small. There are only three items: snow circle, yo-yo, and snow ladder.
8. Strawberry picking is 68 yuan per catty, the price is a little expensive, but the uncle is super nice, please like it.
9. Other hotels, such as doll machines and hand desks, are also very small. The karts next to the hotel have not been tried and have not been evaluated too much.

Overall,
For a parent-child hotel, the place is very big and there are many things, but everything is not perfect. If you choose the season, it is recommended to come in summer and autumn to experience the mountain scenery and farmhouse style. Big expectations.
